                  <form>       
                     <itype>1</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">خَالَ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">خال</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">خالي</orth>
                  </form> is syn. with <foreign lang="ar">ظَنَّ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">تَوَهَّمَ</foreign>: (TA:) you say, <foreign lang="ar">خَالَ الشَّىْءَ</foreign>, (Msb, K,) first pers. <foreign lang="ar">خِلْتُ</foreign>, (JK, S,) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَخَالُ</foreign>, (Msb, K,) first pers. <foreign lang="ar">إِخَالُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">أَخَالُ</foreign>, (JK, S, Msb, K, &amp;c.,) the former irregular, (Msb,) but the more chaste of the two, (S,) and the more used, (Msb,) of the dial. of Teiyi, but commonly used by others also, (El-Marzookee, TA,) the latter of the dial. of Benoo-Asad, accord. to rule, (S, Msb,) but of weak authority, (K,) though some assert it to be the more chaste, (TA,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">خَيْلٌ</foreign> (S, Msb, K) and <foreign lang="ar">خَيْلَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">خِيلٌ</foreign> (K) and <foreign lang="ar">خِيلَةٌ</foreign> (S, K) and <foreign lang="ar">خَالٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">خَيَلَانٌ</foreign>, (K, TA, [the last accord. to the CK <foreign lang="ar">خَيَلَالٌ</foreign>,]) or, as in the T [and JK], <foreign lang="ar">خِيلَانٌ</foreign>, (TA,) and <foreign lang="ar">خَيْلُولَةٌ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">مَخِيلَةٌ</foreign> (S, K) and <foreign lang="ar">مَخَالَةٌ</foreign>; (K;) and <foreign lang="ar">خَالَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">الشَّىْءَ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَخِيلُ</foreign>, is a dial. var. thereof; (Msb;) meaning <foreign lang="ar">ظَنَّةُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">He thought,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">opined, the thing:</hi> and sometimes (see I' Ak p. 109) <hi rend="ital">he knew the thing:</hi> but it seems to have originally signified <foreign lang="ar">توهّم الشىءَ</foreign>, i. e. <hi rend="ital">he surmised,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fancied, the thing:</hi> see <foreign lang="ar">خَالٌ</foreign>, below]. (S, Msb, K.) This verb, being of the class of <foreign lang="ar">ظَنَّ</foreign>, occurs with an inchoative and an enunciative; if commencing the phrase, governing them; but if in the middle or at the end, it may be made to govern or to have no government. (S.) You say, <foreign lang="ar">إِخَالُ زَيْدًا أَخَاكَ</foreign> [and, if you will, <foreign lang="ar">زَيْدٌ إِخَالُ أَخُوكَ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">زَيْدٌ أَخُوكَ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">إِخَالُ</foreign>, <hi rend="ital">I think Zeyd is thy brother</hi> and <hi rend="ital">Zeyd I think is thy brother</hi> and <hi rend="ital">Zeyd is thy brother I think</hi>]. (JK.) Hence the prov., <foreign lang="ar">مَنْ يَسْمَعْ يَخَلْ</foreign>, (S, TA,) i. e. <hi rend="ital">He who hears</hi> the things related of men and of their vices, or faults, <hi rend="ital">will think</hi> evil of them: meaning that it is most safe to keep aloof from other men: or, accord. to some, it is said on the occasion of verifying an opinion. (TA.)       <sense type="A" n="2">-A2-</sense>  See also 8.       <sense type="A" n="3">-A3-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">خال عَلَىالمَالِ</foreign>, aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَخِيلُ</foreign>: see <foreign lang="ar">خَالَ</foreign> in art. <foreign lang="ar">خول</foreign>.       <sense type="A" n="4">-A4-</sense>  <foreign lang="ar">خال</foreign> said of a horse, (JK, K, TA,) aor. <foreign lang="ar">يَخَالُ</foreign>, (K,) inf. n. <foreign lang="ar">خَالٌ</foreign>, (JK, K,) <hi rend="ital">He limped,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">halted,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">was slightly lame.</hi> (JK, K. *)    </entryFree>26:T31f7,<entryFree id="n11865" key="تَخْيِيلٌ" type="main">     
                  <form>       
                     <itype>2</itype>        
                     <orth orig="" extent="full" lang="ar">تَخْيِيلٌ</orth>
                     <orth extent="full" lang="ar">تخييل</orth>
                  </form> signifies The <hi rend="ital">imaging</hi> a thing <hi rend="ital">in the mind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fancying it;</hi> the <hi rend="ital">forming an image,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a fancied image,</hi> thereof <hi rend="ital">in the mind:</hi> (TA:) [and   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-1" target="تَخَيُّلٌ" n="1" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> has the same, as well as a quasipass., signification.] You say, [  
      <foreign lang="ar">خَيَّلْتُهُ <ref cref="n11865-2" target="فَتَخَيَّلَ" n="2" lang="ar" type="7" subtype="WOTF"/> لِى</foreign> and] <foreign lang="ar">لِى</foreign>   
      <foreign lang="ar"><ref cref="n11865-3" target="فَتَخَيَّلَ" n="3" type="0" subtype="FSOSO" lang="ar"/> </foreign>   
      <foreign lang="ar"><ref cref="n11865-4" target="تَخَيَّلْتُهُ" n="4" type="0" subtype="FTFTO" lang="ar"/> </foreign> [<hi rend="ital">I imaged it in the mind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fancied it, and it became imaged in the mind to me,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">an object of fancy to me</hi>]; like as you say, [<foreign lang="ar">صَوَّرْتُهُ فَتَصَوَّرَ لِى</foreign> and] <foreign lang="ar">تَصَوَّرْتُهُ فَتَصَوَّرَ لِى</foreign>: (S:) for   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-5" target="تَخَيُّلٌ" n="5" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar"/></foreign> [as inf. n. of a quasi-pass. verb] signifies a thing's <hi rend="ital">being imaged in the mind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">fancied:</hi> (Er-Rághib, TA:) and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-6" target="تخيّل" n="6" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar" select="n11868"/>الشَّىْءُ لَهُ</foreign> means <foreign lang="ar">تَشَبَّهَ</foreign>. (K. [And the same is indicated in the Msb.]) You say also, <foreign lang="ar">خُيِّلَ لَهُ كَذَا</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Such a thing was imaged to him in the mind;</hi> i. e. <hi rend="ital">such a thing seemed to him</hi>]; from <foreign lang="ar">الوَهْمُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">الظَّنُّ</foreign>: (Msb:) and <foreign lang="ar">خُيِّلَ إِلَيْهِ أَنَّهُ كَذَا</foreign> (S) <hi rend="ital">It was imaged to him</hi> [<hi rend="ital">in the mind,</hi> i. e. <hi rend="ital">it seemed to him,</hi>] <hi rend="ital">that it was so;</hi> syn. <foreign lang="ar">شُبِّهَ</foreign>; (PS;) from <foreign lang="ar">التَّخْيِيلُ</foreign> and <foreign lang="ar">الوَهْمُ</foreign>: (S, TA:) and <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-7" target="تَخَيَّلَ" n="7" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>لَهُ أَنَّهُ كَذَا</foreign> signifies [in like manner <hi rend="ital">it became imaged</hi> &amp;c.; i. e.] <foreign lang="ar">تَشَبَّهَ</foreign>; as also   
      <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-8" target="تخايل" n="8" type="1" subtype="WO" lang="ar" select="n11868"/></foreign>: (S:) and so the first of these three verbs is used in the Kur xx. 69. (TA.) And <foreign lang="ar">فُلَانٌ يَمْضِى عَلَى مَا خَيَّلَتْ</foreign>, (JK and S in explanation of the phrase <foreign lang="ar"> <ref cref="n11865-9" target="عَلَىالمُخَيَّلِ" n="9" type="5" subtype="FSO" lang="ar"/>فُلَانٌ يَمْضِى</foreign>,) i. e. <foreign lang="ar">شَبَّهَتْ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">Such a one goes on, notwithstanding what</hi> (<hi rend="ital">the mind,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">the case,) may image</hi> to him, or <hi rend="ital">what is fancied</hi> by him, of danger of difficulty; <foreign lang="ar">النَّفْسُ</foreign>, or <foreign lang="ar">الحَالُ</foreign>, accord. to Z, (see Freytag's Arab. Prov. ii. 94,) being understood]; meaning, <hi rend="ital">notwithstanding peril,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">risk; without any certain knowledge.</hi> (S.) Whence the prov., <quote>
                     <L>
                        <foreign lang="ar">عَلَىمَا خُيِّلَتْ وَعْثُ القَصِيمِ</foreign>

                  <hi rend="ital">It</hi> (a thing) <hi rend="ital">was,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">became, dubious,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">confused,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">vague,</hi> (JK, S, Mgh, Msb, TA,) <foreign lang="ar">عَلَيْهِ</foreign> 
                  <hi rend="ital">to him.</hi> (JK, Mgh.) One says, <foreign lang="ar">هٰذَا أَمْرٌ لَا</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">يُخِيلُ</foreign> [<hi rend="ital">This is a thing,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">an affair,</hi> or <hi rend="ital">a case, that will not be dubious,</hi> &amp;c.]. (S.) And <foreign lang="ar">لَا يُخِيلُ</foreign> 
                  <foreign lang="ar">ذَاكَ عَلَى أَحَدٍ</foreign>
